<p style="text-align: center;"><a target="_blank" href="https://docs.google.com/document/d/1RLwylAhAqgmwsx_Ejpo_KaiR_Vm1kUNPryD5JiU4BFA/edit?usp=sharing"><span style="font-size: medium;"><strong>Frequently Asked Questions on Weather-Related School Closings/Delays&#160;</strong></span></a></p>
<p style="text-align: center;">&#160;<a href="https://docs.google.com/document/d/1gROSIXByfkQK9YU_sDupEau0d4QUW6hC6cWOJIYV2H8/edit?usp=sharing" style="text-align: center;"><span style="color: rgb(255, 102, 0);">&#160;<strong><span style="font-size: medium;">IMPORTANT: New Automated Call System Information</span></strong></span></a></p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-size: medium;">&#160;</span></p>
<hr />
<div style="color: rgb(34, 34, 34); font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: 12.8px;"><a href="https://docs.google.com/presentation/d/1r86ESoMh9_wkYPtqNf-py4DxjMxVDcYq0roY4psEX5c/preview?slide=id.p" target="_blank" data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&q=https://docs.google.com/presentation/d/1r86ESoMh9_wkYPtqNf-py4DxjMxVDcYq0roY4psEX5c/preview?slide%3Did.p&source=gmail&ust=1515673593940000&usg=AFQjCNFvA6Kf9G9tuaLEf_NMwLFo-nQWAg" style="color: rgb(17, 85, 204);"><span style="color: rgb(255, 102, 0);">State of the District Report</span><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"> - January 8</span></a></div>
<div style="color: rgb(34, 34, 34); font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: 12.8px;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"><br type="_moz" />
</span></div>
<div style="color: rgb(34, 34, 34); font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: 12.8px;"><a href="http://www.yssd.org/LinkClick.aspx?fileticket=z44zXY-iXFo%3d&tabid=6257" target="_blank" data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?hl=en&q=http://www.yssd.org/LinkClick.aspx?fileticket%3Dz44zXY-iXFo%253d%26tabid%3D6257&source=gmail&ust=1515673593940000&usg=AFQjCNExduKEx8eSq8FrSQgbWM2ubbALxw" style="color: rgb(17, 85, 204);"><span style="color: rgb(255, 102, 0);">2018-19 Budget Presentation</span><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"> - January 8</span></a></div>
<div><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">&#160;</span></div>
<hr />
<p>The <a href="https://drive.google.com/file/d/1eVtk6W262Zfcj0QUarj9pff6AIPun9z0/view">2018-19&#160; School Calendar</a> was approved at the November 20 Regular School Board Meeting.</p>
<hr />
<p style="text-align: center;"><a href="http://www.yssd.org/Departments/BusinessOffice/RFPCenter.aspx"><strong><span style="font-size: medium;">York Suburban RFP Center</span></strong></a></p>
<hr />
<p>&#160;&#160;</p>
<p><span style="font-size: small;"> </span></p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><strong><span style="font-size: medium;">York Suburban Community&#160;</span></strong></p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><strong>Information regarding the renovated &#160;stadium and track:</strong></p>
<p style="text-align: center;">&#160;</p>
<p style="text-align: center;">&#160;<strong>&#160;Why is the facility locked?&#160;</strong></p>
<p style="text-align: center;">- to provide a secure teaching environment for all of our students</p>
<p style="text-align: center;">- to prevent vandalism and inappropriate use &#160;&#160;</p>
<p>&#160;</p>
<p style="text-align: center;">&#160;<strong>Why is an annual fee necessary?</strong></p>
<p style="text-align: center;">&#160;&#160;&#160; &#160;The $5 fee is to help offset the expense of access renovation and the additon&#160;&#160;f the electronic security system. Rather than pass on the expense to all taxpayers,&#160;&#160;only the users will be charged the access fee.&#160;York Suburban is committed&#160;to providing an&#160;&#160;open facility for the use of our community&#160;and is the only district to&#160;offer such broad access.&#160;Please review the new&#160;&#160;<a target="_blank" href="https://docs.google.com/document/d/17eXi2bHxv_h-CnGsBJhAi6MrN3k1n1y6Cbs7aVm1WP4/edit">GUIDELINES and PROCESS</a>&#160;&#160;for community access.&#160;&#160; Thank you!</p>
<p style="text-align: center;">&#160;</p>
<hr />
<p style="text-align: center;"><span style="text-align: left; font-family: Arial;"><span style="color: rgb(255, 102, 0);"><span style="font-size: medium;">&#160; &#160; NEW&#160;</span></span></span><span style="text-align: left; color: rgb(255, 102, 0);"><strong><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-family: Arial;">YSHS&#160;</span></span></strong></span><span style="text-align: left; color: rgb(255, 102, 0);"><span style="font-size: medium;"><a target="_blank" href="http://www.yssd.org/Buildings/HighSchool/Athletics.aspx"><span style="color: rgb(255, 102, 0);"><strong><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-family: Arial;">ATHLETIC EVENT ADMITTANCE POLICY</span></span></strong></span></a></span></span>&#160; &#160; &#160; &#160; &#160; &#160; &#160; &#160; &#160; &#160; &#160; &#160; &#160; &#160; &#160; &#160; &#160; &#160; &#160; &#160; &#160; &#160; &#160; &#160; &#160;<span style="font-size: medium;">&#160; &#160; &#160;</span><span style="font-size: medium;">&#160; &#160; &#160; &#160; &#160; &#160; &#160; &#160; &#160; &#160; &#160; &#160; &#160; &#160; &#160; &#160; &#160; &#160; &#160; &#160; &#160; &#160; &#160;</span>&#160;</p>

<h1 class="ProfileHeaderCard-name" style="font-size: 24px; margin: 0px; text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; line-height: 1; color: rgb(41, 47, 51); font-family: Arial, sans-serif; background-color: rgb(245, 248, 250); text-align: center;"><img src="/Portals/0/staff/jhershner/impact.png" width="300" height="60" alt="" /></h1>
<div>&#160;</div>
<p>&#160;</p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><span style="color: rgb(136, 153, 166); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; white-space: nowrap;"><a href="https://twitter.com/YSImpactFdn" class="twitter-follow-button" data-show-count="false">Follow @YSImpactFdn</a><script async src="//platform.twitter.com/widgets.js" charset="utf-8"></script></span></p>

		<p>&#160;</p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><img src="/Portals/0/MCF2018image.PNG" width="175" height="111" alt="" /></p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><img src="/Portals/0/MCF2018.PNG" width="447" height="177" alt="" /></p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Comic Sans MS&quot;;"><span style="color: rgb(255, 102, 0);"><a href="/LinkClick.aspx?fileticket=b_tw-fcIwyY%3d&tabid=57" target="_blank">MORE INFO</a></span></span>&#160;</p>
<hr />
<p style="color: rgb(57, 57, 57); font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; border: 0px; text-align: center;">&#160;</p>
<p style="color: rgb(57, 57, 57); font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; border: 0px; text-align: center;">&#160;<img src="/Portals/0/staff/jhershner/BHSummerCamp.PNG" width="399" height="141" alt="" /></p>
<p style="text-align: center;">Click here for <a href="/LinkClick.aspx?fileticket=nIj2l5Xs98w%3d&tabid=57" target="_blank">Summer Camp Information</a></p>
<p style="text-align: center;">&#160;</p>
<hr />
<p style="text-align: center;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;<img src="/Portals/0/staff/jhershner/whitsons2.PNG" width="189" height="163" alt="" />&#160;</p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-size: small;">Did you kn</span><span style="font-size: small;">ow that school breakfast is served in all YS cafeterias each day??</span></p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-size: small;">Breakfast is included with free/reduced meal benefits - and eating breakfast improves concentration, alertness, comprehension, memory, and learning!</span></p>
<p style="text-align: center;">&#160;</p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><strong><span style="font-size: small;">&#160;<span style="color: rgb(20, 23, 26); font-family: &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; letter-spacing: 0.27px; white-space: pre-wrap;">Full time position available with Whitsons at YSHS. To apply visit </span></span></strong><font color="#14171a" face="Segoe UI, Arial, sans-serif" size="2"><span style="letter-spacing: 0.27px; white-space: pre-wrap;"><a href="http://whitsons.com/index.php/career/careers-center" target="_blank"><strong>Whitsons Career Center</strong></a></span></font><strong><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="color: rgb(20, 23, 26); font-family: &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; letter-spacing: 0.27px; white-space: pre-wrap;"> (requisition # 5032)</span></span></strong></p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-size: medium;"><img src="/Portals/0/staff/jhershner/whitsons breakfast.jpg" width="259" height="194" alt="" /></span></p>
<p style="text-align: center;">&#160;</p>
<hr />
<p style="text-align: center;">&#160;</p>
<p style="text-align: left;">&#160;</p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><a target="_blank" href="http://paschoolperformance.org/"><img width="150" hspace="3" height="84" border="0" align="top" src="/Portals/0/images/PSPP.PNG" style="border: 0px;" alt="" /></a></p>
<p>&#160;</p>
<p><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-family: Arial;"> </span></span></p>
<p><a target="_blank" href="http://paschoolperformance.org/"><strong>The York Suburban School District would like to share their PA School Performance Profile scores.</strong></a></p>
<p>&#160;</p>
<p><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-family: Arial;">&#160;&#160;</span></span></p>

<p style="text-align: left;"><a href="http://www.k12paymentcenter.com" target="_blank">&#160;A new online meal payment system, K12 Payment Center is now available to deposit funds into your student's account and get a report on purchases.</a></p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><a href="http://www.k12paymentcenter.com" target="_blank" name="K12 Payment Center Link"><img src="/Portals/0/images/K12PaymentCenter.PNG" width="150" height="21" alt="K12 Payment Center Logo" /></a></p>
